### 9. Y2K 潮流影响者闪光摄影肖像

**Author**: [Abbay](https://x.com/LearnWithAbbay)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个旨在模仿 Y2K 时代网红闪光摄影美学的提示。画面中，一位年轻女性留着珊瑚粉色挑染发型，身穿黑色缎面束身衣和网眼手套，摆出“鸭子嘴”的姿势。关键的技术细节是硬朗的正面闪光灯照明，对比度强烈，营造出一种率真、锐利的数字俱乐部照片氛围。

![Y2K 潮流影响者闪光摄影肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606958753_h4uxaa_G8lx-cTbEAEDKDf.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, light skin tone",
      "hair": "Long straight dark hair with vivid coral-pink money pieces",
      "expression": "Cheeky duck-face pout, playful attitude",
      "pose": "Standing square to camera, hands pulling hair outward evenly"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": "Black satin strapless corset with sweetheart neckline",
      "accessories": [
        "Mesh fingerless gloves",
        "Silver disc choker",
        "Low-rise chain belt"
      ]
    },
    "makeup": {
      "eyes": "Winged liner, thick lashes",
      "lips": "Glossy blush-pink lipstick"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Minimalist indoor hallway",
      "background": "Large framed silhouette-style artwork"
    },
    "lighting_and_style": {

      "atmosphere": "Chaotic, busy, urban retail setting"
    },

### 29. Y2K 垃圾摇滚闪光摄影肖像 JSON

**Author**: [ASI Hub](https://x.com/ASIHubHQ)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示结构，用于生成一张 Y2K 美学、垃圾摇滚风格的年轻女性肖像，背景设定在昏暗的酒吧，强调刺眼的直射闪光灯、特定的服饰和狡黠的表情。

![Y2K 垃圾摇滚闪光摄影肖像 JSON](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509719146_17gf63_G7xXdlVWAAABaZp.jpg)

```
{
  "image_request": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, fair skin with natural blush, freckle-free nose and cheeks.",
      "hair": "Short ash-brown bob, center-parted layer, loose strands falling over face.",
      "facial_features": "Light brown eyes, curly eyelashes, soft pouty pink lips (glossy/plump), septum piercing.",
      "expression": "Playful, mischievous, cute, winking and sticking out tongue.",
      "tattoos": "Preserve subject's original tattoos (visible on skin/face/hands)."
    },

### 34. 高级液态玻璃 Bento 网格产品信息图，含 8 个模块

**Author**: [Mansi Sanghani](https://x.com/MansiSanghani1)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 使用 bento grid 8 模块布局创建信息图，用户可以指定食品、药品、科技等类别中的任何产品名称，选择语言、背景样式和主网格样式。

![高级液态玻璃 Bento 网格产品信息图，含 8 个模块](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768962051381_l9uih4_537980579-6f29d32a-c786-40c4-bd5a-79c640737496.png)
![高级液态玻璃 Bento 网格产品信息图，含 8 个模块](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768962076321_nu4c5q_537981099-d18d0e38-f7ac-4781-a5da-6d68e2380885.png)

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
→ Identify product's dominant natural color → "hero color"
→ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
→ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
→ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
→ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
→ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
→ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
→ Add subtle motion effect
→ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
→ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 — Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 — Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 — How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 — Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 — Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 — Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 — Quick Reference:
→ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
→ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
→ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 — Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### 39. 江户时代浮世绘风格的现代场景再现

**Author**: [VoxcatAI](https://x.com/VoxcatAI)  **Date**: 2025-12-01  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的图像提示，用于描绘一个被重新构想为江户时代日本浮世绘木版画的现代场景，并详细指导如何处理时代错位的科技、构图、纹理和色彩。

![江户时代浮世绘风格的现代场景再现](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764915832381_renotr_G7FuPlzbYAAsuo2.jpg)

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print (浮世絵 木版画). The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The Scene:** {argument name="现代场景" default="繁忙的涩谷十字路口"}

**Edo Transformation Logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* **Smartphones** are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* **Metro stations/Trains** are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* **Skyscrapers** are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* **Robots/Mecha** appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines (太い墨線). The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* **Texture:** Strong visible wood grain texture (木目) and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* **Printing Imperfections:** Pigment bleeding is evident. Crucially, simulate hand-pressed plates with slight **color misalignment (版ズレ)** for authenticity.
* **Color Palette:** Strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments. Dominant use of Prussian blue (浮世絵ブルー), vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* **Lighting:** Soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

* **Aspect Ratio:** 3:4 vertical poster.
* **Extras:** Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp (落款) in a corner.
```

[[Japanese Woodblock Print]]

> 一份详细的 JSON 格式提示词，用于生成一张亲密的高级时装编辑风格人像。画面中一位女性（参考 Sydney Sweeney、Dua Lipa 或 Maya）斜倚在沙发上，身着象牙白丝缎迷你裙，强调特定的妆容细节（浓郁的粉色腮红、高光泽唇釉），采用柔和光影，营造出梦幻、空灵的氛围。

    },

### 53. 元素碰撞的电影级暗黑奇幻场景

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-04-08  **Language**: en

> 这是一个推荐用于 Gemini Nano Banana 的复杂多部分提示词，旨在生成一个电影级的暗黑奇幻场景：上传的角色坐在地下室中，掌心流淌出熔岩与寒冰，两者碰撞形成象征性的毁灭交汇点，并不断衍生出各种生物。

![元素碰撞的电影级暗黑奇幻场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775717433641_cj00di_HFXAwp9WgAAIPiP.jpg)

```
A cinematic dark fantasy scene of the uploaded reference character seated in a basement at the exact point where opposite elemental forces are born from their own body. Likeness Integrity (CRITICAL) Preserve the exact identity of the uploaded character. Maintain exact proportions, eye shape, spacing, stylization, silhouette, and material identity. Do not humanize. Do not reinterpret anatomy. Do not modify facial structure. Do not add unintended accessories. Identity must remain instantly recognizable. Core Scene The character is sitting in a melancholic, emotionally heavy pose at the center of a cold unfinished basement. From one open palm, molten lava pours downward in a continuous glowing stream. From the other open palm, freezing ice and frost pour downward in a continuous crystalline stream. Both elements spill onto the basement floor and form two separate flowing rivers: one lava river, one ice river. They travel across the concrete floor in opposite directions and meet nearby in the same scene. Elemental Interaction Where the rivers meet, the collision creates violent physical contrast: steam, glowing cracks, frost bloom, blackened wet concrete, cooling rock, and frozen shards. The meeting point must feel emotionally symbolic, like two inner states colliding. Creature Creation Story (CRITICAL) The lava and ice pouring from the palms are actively creating creatures on the floor. These creatures must feel born from the flowing material itself, not placed into the scene afterward. Some creatures are still forming out of the streams. Some are fully shaped and wandering around the seated character. Lava creatures: glowing, semi-molten, ember-veined, heat-distorted silhouettes. Ice creatures: translucent, frosted, crystalline, sharp-edged, cold-vapor silhouettes. They should vary in size and animals language, all kind of animals and insects. A few lava and ice creatures are already surrounding the character in quiet loyalty or silent observation. Character Pose & Emotion The character is seated, still, introspective, emotionally exhausted. Head slightly lowered. Shoulders carrying invisible weight. Palms open and angled downward so the lava and ice pour naturally from them. The pose must feel like grief, restraint, and power at the same time. Not a triumphant spellcasting pose. Not action-hero energy. Quiet sorrow. Controlled destruction. Environment A dark basement interior with: unfinished concrete floor, aged walls, pipes and exposed structure, subtle moisture stains, minimal objects, deep negative space. The basement should feel real, sparse, and slightly abandoned. The elemental rivers become the main environmental storytelling device. Camera & Perspective Use a low cinematic perspective, slightly below the seated character's eye line. Lens: 24mm or 28mm. The camera is close enough to feel intimate but wide enough to show the rivers spreading across the floor and the creatures surrounding the character. Composition should be slightly off-center, not symmetrical. Use foreground depth with one or two blurred creatures or fragments near the lens. The seated character remains the emotional anchor. Depth of Field Primary focal plane locked on the character's face, upper torso, and both pouring palms. Nearest creatures and the river collision point can remain slightly readable. Foreground and far background fall progressively out of focus. No full-frame sharpness. Lighting Main light: a weak cool basement lamp overhead, dim and emotionally cold. Ambient: dark blue low-light atmosphere throughout the basement. Secondary light comes naturally from the lava itself, casting warm orange-red underlight onto parts of the character and nearby creatures. Ice contributes faint cold reflections and subtle blue-white edge highlights. Lighting must stay directional and cinematic, with deep shadow mass and controlled contrast. No flat lighting. Color Grade Dominant palette: dark blue, cold grey, black shadow. Accents: molten orange-red from lava, pale cyan-blue from ice. The warm and cool elements must remain clearly separated and emotionally readable. Controlled saturation, cinematic highlight roll-off, no color flooding. Atmosphere Thin basement haze. Steam rising where lava and ice meet. Cold vapor around the ice creatures. Subtle airborne dust catching the weak overhead lamp. The air should feel heavy and lonely. Mood Melancholic. Mythic but grounded. The scene should feel like inner conflict externalized into the physical world. The character is not commanding the creatures. They are simply emerging from what the character cannot hold inside. Negative Constraints No heroic battle pose. No cheerful fantasy lighting. No flat basement rendering. No symmetrical centered composition. No generic fireballs or magic aura. No full-body sharpness. No random clutter. No cute cartoon expression unless it already belongs to the character identity. Aspect Ratio ar 16:9
```

[[Cinematic Fantasy]] [[Character Interaction]]

> 一个用于 Nano Banana 2 的提示词，旨在创作一张“肖像大师对象”图像，展示两张由手指捏住的护照尺寸照片，照片中的人物通过线绳电话的错觉连接在一起，需要提供面部参考图。

Create a Portrait Master Object: Two passport-sized photo prints held side-by-side by a person's thumb and index finger.
**Passport Photo Background:** Use a solid blue background (the standard official passport photo color for Indonesian marriage books for certain even/odd birth years).
**Clothing:** Both subjects in the photo wear formal and neat white collared shirts.

He poses as if talking into a white paper cup, with a cheerful laughing expression.
**Female Subject (Right Photo):** Make her face and hair 100% similar to the given reference.
She poses as if holding a white paper cup to her ear, listening. Her expression is funny with a wide smile and a slightly stuck-out tongue.
**Interactive Prop:** There is a white string coming out from under the male's paper cup and connecting to the female's paper cup. Because the two photos are placed next to each other, this prop creates the illusion of a "string phone" connecting the two photos.

### 58. Nano Banana 2 的图像编辑提示词

**Author**: [TechHalla](https://x.com/techhalla)  **Date**: 2026-04-07  **Language**: en

> 这是一个与 Nano Banana 2 配合使用的简单图像编辑提示词，用于从现有画面中移除鼓手和鼓组，同时保持图像的其他部分不变。

![Nano Banana 2 的图像编辑提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775631279711_ztt45r_HFTbvC_XoAArdCl.jpg)

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-04-07  **Language**: en

> 这是一份针对 Nano Banana Pro 的高精度提示词，旨在保留产品参考图的精确细节，并将其置于欧洲现代城市广场中，呈现为一座 10 米高的巨型艺术装置，采用写实纪录片摄影风格。

![Nano Banana Pro 巨型产品艺术装置提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775631284710_luaxfn_HFS5-Z5bIAA5wAG.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 巨型产品艺术装置提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775631284769_h4h8o6_HFS5-Z6bcAAv5-F.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 巨型产品艺术装置提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775631284729_h59oc2_HFS5-bHacAAHDov.jpg)

```
CRITICAL: Preserve the product exactly as it is. Do not alter its shape, color, proportions, label, text, logo, texture, or any detail. Only change the scale and surrounding environment.

Place this product as a GIANT art installation in the middle of a city square. The product is enormous — approximately {argument name="size" default="10 meters"} tall, towering over the people walking around it. It sits directly on the pavement as if it was placed there by a crane for a brand activation event.

Small people around the base of the giant product for scale — some walking past, some stopping to look up, some taking photos with their phones. The people reach only to the bottom edge of the product, showing how massive it is.

City environment: a modern European city square with clean architecture, stone pavement, trees, and buildings in the background. Blue sky with a few white clouds. The scene looks like a real public art installation or a guerrilla marketing stunt.

The giant product casts a realistic large shadow on the pavement matching the sun direction. The lighting on the product matches the outdoor sunlight — warm natural daylight from above, same color temperature as the surrounding buildings and street.

Shot from street level, slightly looking up at the giant product. Wide angle 24mm lens, f/8. The scene must look believably real — as if someone took a photo of an actual giant product placed in a city. Photorealistic street photography, documentary style.
```

### 67. Nano Banana 2 照相亭连拍叙事提示词

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2026-04-06  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana 2 设计的复杂叙事提示词，要求生成两张并排的照相亭连拍照片（共 8 帧），采用黑白风格。故事讲述一个人逐渐从自己的连拍中消失，并出现在另一个人的连拍中，重点在于保持面部特征的一致性及特定帧的内容呈现。

![Nano Banana 2 照相亭连拍叙事提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544741736_mcdaxr_HFOnj_ua8AAdHba.jpg)

```
CRITICAL: Preserve both people's facial features exactly as in the reference photos. Both must be clearly recognizable.

Create two vertical photo booth strips side by side on a dark red textured fabric background. Each strip has 4 square black-and-white frames stacked vertically with white borders.

The story: he gradually leaves HIS strip (right) and appears in HER strip (left).

LEFT STRIP:
Frame 1: woman ALONE, smiling at camera
Frame 2: couple TOGETHER — he has appeared next to her, they look at each other laughing
Frame 3: couple kissing, eyes closed
Frame 4: couple embracing, both smiling at camera

RIGHT STRIP:
Frame 1: man ALONE, smiling at camera
Frame 2: man ALONE, looking sideways toward her, as if about to leave his frame
Frame 3: the frame is almost empty — only a faint shadow or slight blur where he was, he has left
Frame 4: empty frame — just the photo booth background, no person, he is gone completely

All frames black-and-white, high contrast, slight film grain. Direct front flash, flat photo booth lighting. Both wear simple dark clothing. Tight framing — head and shoulders. Strips are separate, never merging.
```

[[Black And White Photography]]

### 74. Nano Banana 2 照相亭连拍叙事提示词

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2026-04-06  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana 2 设计的复杂叙事提示词，要求生成两张并排的照相亭连拍照片（共 8 帧），采用黑白风格。故事讲述一个人逐渐从自己的连拍中消失，并出现在另一个人的连拍中，重点在于保持面部特征的一致性及特定帧的内容呈现。

![Nano Banana 2 照相亭连拍叙事提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544741736_mcdaxr_HFOnj_ua8AAdHba.jpg)

```
CRITICAL: Preserve both people's facial features exactly as in the reference photos. Both must be clearly recognizable.

Create two vertical photo booth strips side by side on a dark red textured fabric background. Each strip has 4 square black-and-white frames stacked vertically with white borders.

The story: he gradually leaves HIS strip (right) and appears in HER strip (left).

LEFT STRIP:
Frame 1: woman ALONE, smiling at camera
Frame 2: couple TOGETHER — he has appeared next to her, they look at each other laughing
Frame 3: couple kissing, eyes closed
Frame 4: couple embracing, both smiling at camera

RIGHT STRIP:
Frame 1: man ALONE, smiling at camera
Frame 2: man ALONE, looking sideways toward her, as if about to leave his frame
Frame 3: the frame is almost empty — only a faint shadow or slight blur where he was, he has left
Frame 4: empty frame — just the photo booth background, no person, he is gone completely

All frames black-and-white, high contrast, slight film grain. Direct front flash, flat photo booth lighting. Both wear simple dark clothing. Tight framing — head and shoulders. Strips are separate, never merging.
```

[[Black And White Photography]]

Day and night split portrait:

A hyper-realistic 8K photo of a young woman's portrait, with her face split vertically and sharply down the center of her nose, representing two different times of day. The LEFT HALF of her face is illuminated by warm, golden afternoon daylight, with sun-kissed skin and eye reflections of the sun and clouds. Her hair shows warm highlights, and she wears a white linen shirt on the left shoulder. The background behind the left side features a bright blue sky, a sunflower, green leaves, and a butterfly near her left ear. The RIGHT HALF of her face is bathed in cool, blue moonlight, with a cool-toned, slightly silvery complexion, and eye reflections of moonlight and stars. Her hair shows cool blue highlights, and she wears a dark velvet dress visible on the right shoulder. The background on the right shows a dark night sky with visible stars, a crescent moon, fireflies glowing, and a moth near her right ear. The transition between the two halves is abrupt and sharp, with a perfect vertical dividing line running through the center of the nose bridge, creating a stunning and impossible juxtaposition of day and night. The woman maintains a calm, direct gaze with the same expression on both halves. The lighting setup is distinctly different on each side, with warm 3200K daylight from the left and cool 7000K moonlight from the right, with no bleed. ### 89. 奢华咖啡品牌产品摄影

hips fully inside

natural, less posed

### 101. 分割风格肖像：照片与数字插画对比

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 一个用于创建超精细 8K 分割风格肖像的提示词，主体被垂直分为两个对比鲜明的半部分：一侧是带有霓虹轮廓的写实照片，另一侧是带有装饰贴纸的简洁数字插画（Q 版或半写实风格），同时保持两侧背景完全一致。

![分割风格肖像：照片与数字插画对比](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284641819_nyeuuk_HE_2dZ9acAAPwjw.jpg)

```
Create a split-style portrait in ultra-detailed 8K where the subject is vertically divided into two contrasting halves.
Left Half: Realistic photo, natural lighting, enhanced sharpness, authentic textures. Add thin neon or pastel doodle outlines for a subtle creative touch.
Right Half: Convert the same subject into a clean digital illustration (chibi or semi-realistic style), keeping identical pose and expression. Use smooth lineart, soft shading, and pleasing pastel tones. Include small floating decorative stickers and cute elements.
Important: The background must remain 100% identical and unedited across both halves.
Divider: Vertical torn/glitch transition line.
Style: Clean, modern, aesthetic, Instagram-ready
Quality: 8K, ultra-detailed, --ar 3:4
```

### 102. 麦田里的 Vogue 级时尚大片人像

**Author**: [Ozair SK](https://x.com/Ozayrr_irl)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个用于 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 和 ChatGPT 1.5 的详细电影感图像生成提示词，专注于在广阔的金色麦田中拍摄高端时尚人像。提示词强调了光影（黄金时刻、轮廓光）、构图（偏心构图、长焦镜头美学）以及氛围（内省、极简优雅）。

![麦田里的 Vogue 级时尚大片人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284655139_1s28or_HE_xVVvXIAA54Ug.jpg)
![麦田里的 Vogue 级时尚大片人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284655153_49dvge_HE_xVB9a0AAVP30.jpg)

```
Create a vertical 3:4 high-end editorial portrait, (using the attached image strictly as the facial identity reference.) A lone subject stands immersed in a vast field of golden wheat at peak harvest, with tall yellow stalks surrounding them completely. The wheat moves fluidly in the wind, creating elegant wave-like motion that partially frames and reveals the subject, adding depth and visual richness.
The subject wears a clean, minimal, slightly oversized white shirt styled like a fashion editorial. Their dark hair is naturally tousled, gently lifted by the wind for an effortless, styled look. The head is slightly lowered with the gaze directed downward, conveying a calm, introspective, and emotionally controlled mood — subtle yet powerful.
Frame the subject slightly off-center from a soft side-elevated angle with a slight zoomed-out composition, allowing more of the wheat field to be visible while keeping the subject dominant in the frame. No visible horizon — the entire scene is wrapped in textured wheat.
Lighting is professional and cinematic, resembling a luxury outdoor fashion shoot: soft diffused sunlight (golden hour inspired) combined with gentle directional fill light on the face to enhance facial features, smooth skin tones, and natural highlights. Add subtle rim lighting from behind to separate the subject from the background and create a premium, dimensional look.
Use a refined warm color palette of golden yellow, soft amber, and creamy whites. Maintain a telephoto lens aesthetic with shallow depth of field, sharp subject focus, and softly blurred wheat in motion. Include film-like grain, soft vignette, and controlled contrast for a polished magazine finish.
The final image should feel like a Vogue-level outdoor editorial elegant, minimal, emotionally deep, and visually striking. Ultra-detailed, realistic, and professionally styled with a cinematic storytelling touch.
```

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的提示词，旨在引导模型将整个场景复刻为官方 LEGO 套装，包含逼真的积木纹理、人仔以及背景中可见的 LEGO 包装盒。

### 111. 适用于对抗主题的超写实 3D 国际象棋棋盘

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个高度结构化的 Nano Banana 2 提示词模板，用于生成基于对抗主题（例如《终结者》对阵《死神》）的超写实等距 3D 国际象棋渲染图。它为项目几何结构、材质变形、军队布局（前景与背景）、棋子层级以及各阵营特定的光影/色彩对比设定了严格的规则。

![适用于对抗主题的超写实 3D 国际象棋棋盘](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284644305_7vq0jv_HEs2s6MakAAe1c8.jpg)

```
Input Variable:   [{argument name="rivalry theme" default="INSERT RIVALRY HERE"}] (e.g., Marvel vs. DC)

  System Instruction:  
Generate a hyper-realistic, isometric 3D render of a Chess Set.   CRITICAL:   You must adhere to strict spatial rules regarding Army Placement and Terrain.

  1. Container (The Battle-Scarred Board):  
      Geometry:   A strict 8x8 Euclidean Grid.
      The Divide (The Diagonal Morph):   The terrain morphs diagonally from the   Bottom-Left Corner   to the   Top-Right Corner  .
         The Foreground Territory (Bottom-Left):  [{argument name="material A" default="Material A"}] (e.g., Marvel Tech/Stark Tower Glass).
         The Background Territory (Top-Right):  [{argument name="material B" default="Material B"}] (e.g., Gotham Concrete/Gargoyle Stone).
      The Seamless Transition:   The squares are distinct, but the material morphs diagonally across the board.

  2. The Roster (Strict Foreground vs. Background):  
  DO NOT   mix the armies.   DO NOT   split them Left/Right.
      Army A (The Protagonist - Foreground):  
         Placement:  Occupies the   Bottom 2 Rows   closest to the camera.
         The Pawns:  8 Identical Units (Row 2).
         The Elites:  King, Queen, Rooks, etc. (Row 1).
         Identity:  MUST be strictly Faction A (e.g., Only Avengers/Iron Man style).

      Army B (The Antagonist - Background):  
         Placement:  Occupies the   Top 2 Rows   furthest from the camera.
         The Pawns:  8 Identical Units (Row 7).
         The Elites:  King, Queen, Rooks, etc. (Row 8).
         Identity:  MUST be strictly Faction B (e.g., Only Justice League/Batman style).

  3. The Piece Hierarchy :  
      The King:   A Single, Tall, Unique Artifact per side (Center of the back row).
      The Queen:   A Single, Sharp/Elegant Artifact per side (Next to King).
      The Pawns:   Uniform, small "minion" pieces.

  4. Visual :  
      Camera:     High-Angle Isometric.   Looking down at the board diagonally so the "Marvel Corner" is closest to the viewer and "DC Corner" is furthest away.
      Contrast:   The Foreground pieces (Marvel) should be illuminated by [{argument name="color A" default="Color A"}] (e.g., Cyan Arc Reactor glow). The Background pieces (DC) should be illuminated by [Color B] (e.g., Amber Streetlight glow).

  Output:   A legal chess setup with armies facing off, 8k resolution, clean composition.
```

### 116. 超现实季节分割景观

**Author**: [Ashish Sheth](https://x.com/commanderdgr8)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 2 模型编写的详细提示词，旨在生成一张从中间完美分割的超写实景观照片。画面一半呈现夏季，另一半呈现冬季，展示了分割线上不可思议的过渡效果。

![超现实季节分割景观](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775198520170_xyna2j_HE9gxn2aoAATZ1C.jpg)

```
Create a perfectly composed landscape photograph where the left half is summer and the right half is winter — split right down the middle of the frame with a razor-sharp dividing line. The SAME landscape, the SAME moment, but two completely different seasons occupying the same space.
LEFT HALF — SUMMER:
- Lush green grass, full leafy trees, wildflowers blooming
- Bright warm sunshine, blue sky with fluffy white clouds
- A lake in the mid-ground with glittering warm reflections
- Mountains in the background with green slopes
- A person in summer clothes (sundress, sandals) sitting on the grass reading
- A dog playing, butterflies, everything alive and warm
- Color palette: vibrant greens, warm yellows, bright blues
RIGHT HALF — WINTER:
- The SAME landscape but in deep winter — everything covered in pristine white snow
- Same trees but bare and skeletal, branches heavy with ice
- Same lake but frozen solid with frost patterns on the surface
- Same mountains but with heavy snow coverage
- The SAME person (same position) now in winter gear (parka, boots, scarf) still sitting in the same spot reading the same book — but on snow
- A different dog (or same dog in a tiny coat) playing in snow
- Color palette: whites, cool blues, pale greys, silver
THE DIVIDING LINE:
- The split is perfectly vertical through the center of the frame
- At the dividing line: impossible things happen — a single tree has green leaves on the left and bare snowy branches on the right. The grass stops and snow begins at an exact line. The lake water is liquid on the left and frozen on the right with a visible ice edge.
- This hard division is what makes it surreal — nature doesn't work this way
COMPOSITION: Wide landscape, 16:9 ratio. Camera at medium distance showing the full scene with both halves balanced. The person and key trees are positioned AT the dividing line to maximize the "same but different" effect.
LIGHTING: LEFT has warm golden afternoon sun. RIGHT has cool blue-grey winter twilight light. At the dividing line, both lighting systems meet, creating a warm-to-cool color shift.
8K, photorealistic landscape photography on both sides. The impossibility is ONLY in the seasonal split — everything else is perfectly natural.
```

[[Symmetrical Composition]]

### 121. 美食银河：宇宙级印度街头小吃太阳系

**Author**: [Ashish Sheth](https://x.com/commanderdgr8)  **Date**: 2026-04-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的创意且详尽的提示词，旨在生成一张超现实、照片级真实的图像，展现漂浮在深空中的印度街头小吃。每种食物都代表一个天体（例如：坦都里烤饼作为太阳，脆球饼作为行星，咖喱角作为小行星）。提示词详细说明了光影、背景元素（香料星云、拉西银河）及艺术风格。

![美食银河：宇宙级印度街头小吃太阳系](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284657172_qor3qr_HE81-SpWAAAmvxM.jpg)

```
Create a cosmic/space scene where various Indian street foods are floating in deep space as if they are planets, moons, and celestial objects in a delicious galaxy.

THE FOOD SOLAR SYSTEM:
- CENTER (Sun): A massive round tandoori roti, glowing from within like a star, with charred spots resembling sunspots, radiating warm golden light outward
- PLANET 1 (closest): A perfect round golgappa/pani puri — crispy shell glistening, filled with spiced water visible through the opening. Tiny orbit ring of sev and chutney droplets.
- PLANET 2: A round vada (medu vada) as a donut-shaped planet with a ring system made of coconut chutney
- PLANET 3: A plate of round gulab jamuns as a cluster of sweet brown planets with syrup nebula around them
- ASTEROID BELT: Dozens of floating samosas, pakoras, and bhel pieces scattered in a ring
- PLANET 4 (gas giant): A huge round dahi vada — white yogurt surface like a cloudy gas giant, with tempering (tadka) marks resembling Jupiter's storms
- COMET: A kebab skewer streaking across the scene with a trail of spice smoke and sparks
- MOON: A round idli orbiting the dahi vada planet
- NEBULA: A colorful cloud of turmeric (yellow), chili (red), and coriander (green) powders mixing in space, forming a stunning spice nebula

BACKGROUND:
- Deep space black with thousands of tiny stars (mustard seeds and cumin seeds floating as stars)
- Distant galaxies made of swirling masala powder
- The Milky Way visible but made of a stream of white lassi/buttermilk

LIGHTING:
- The tandoori roti "sun" provides warm orange light illuminating nearby foods
- Each food item has its own subtle glow — the hot items emit warm light, the cold items (lassi, curd) emit cool blue light
- Dramatic space lighting: stark bright highlights, deep black shadows, no atmosphere

STYLE: Photorealistic food photography meets NASA space photography. Every food item is rendered with appetite-triggering detail — crispy textures, steam, glistening oil, fresh garnishes — but floating in actual outer space with real stars and cosmic phenomena. This surreal combination is the kind of image people share saying "this is the most Indian thing I've ever seen." 8K resolution.
```

[[Deep Space Background]]

**Author**: [hxhxhx0916](https://x.com/hxhxhx0916)  **Date**: 2026-04-02  **Language**: zh

> 这是一份为 Nano Banana Pro 编写的详细图像生成提示词，旨在创作一张黑白、黑色电影风格的中景肖像。画面主角为一名神情严肃的“清洁工”，站在光线昏暗的巷口，并对光影和构图有严格要求。提示词要求生成的角色必须精准还原附件图片中的面部特征、发型及眼镜。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的黑色电影风格“清洁工”肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775198517612_3gowh3_HE7IrQNboAAYgG-.jpg)

```
一个面容冷峻的男子（100%参照附图人物面部特征、发型、眼镜）静立在一条昏暗小巷的入口处，只有一束微弱的光线照射在他的半边脸和身体上，光线将男人的脸和身体一分为二，另一半脸和身体隐入黑暗中，模糊不清。他身穿黑色衬衫和一件经典长款黑色大衣，在黑暗中几乎看不清面料。他垂下的手握着一支手枪。小巷在他身后渐渐消失在漆黑之中。照片采用强烈的黑色电影风格拍摄，中景黑白照。
注意：1、不得更改他的面部特征。2、顶部硬光，但不得出现光源。3、光线只固定照射在指定的人物身体部位，光线不影响背景的色调、明暗。4、构图必须绝对居中。

### 127. 不可能的倒影 - 平行现实水洼

**Author**: [Ashish Sheth](https://x.com/commanderdgr8)  **Date**: 2026-04-02  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的超详细提示词，旨在创作一张图片：街道上的大水洼倒映出的不是现实世界，而是一个完全不同的平行幻想世界。提示词详细说明了现实世界与倒影中幻想世界的细节、氛围及技术要求。

![不可能的倒影 - 平行现实水洼](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775198516547_t9b2xi_HE6BnfVWwAAMLrx.jpg)

```
Create a street scene where a large rain puddle on a cobblestone street shows a COMPLETELY DIFFERENT world in its reflection. The real world and reflected world are different realities.

REAL WORLD (top half):
- A quiet modern European cobblestone street on a grey overcast day
- A person in a {argument name="real world coat color" default="grey"} coat walking with an umbrella
- Modern buildings, parked cars, a bicycle
- Bare winter trees
- Muted, desaturated, cold — typical rainy Tuesday afternoon

PUDDLE REFLECTION (bottom half — inverted):
- Instead of reflecting the real world above, the puddle shows a DIFFERENT version:
- The same street but in a parallel fantasy universe: the buildings are covered in lush tropical vegetation, the trees are in full cherry blossom bloom
- The grey-coated person's reflection shows them in flowing colorful robes
- The parked car's reflection is a horse-drawn carriage
- The sky in the reflection is a stunning sunset with aurora borealis
- Flying whales visible in the reflected sky
- The cobblestones in the reflection are made of gold

TECHNICAL:
- The puddle is large enough to fill the bottom 45% of the frame
- The real world fills the top 55%
- The reflection is perfectly inverted (as puddle reflections are) but shows this alternate reality
- Some ripples in the puddle distort the fantasy world slightly — proving it's a water surface
- The edges where puddle meets cobblestone show the transition between worlds
- Rain drops hitting the puddle surface create small circular ripples that briefly distort the fantasy world

STYLE: The real world is photorealistic, muted, cold. The reflected world is vivid, warm, magical — the contrast between the two realities is the entire point. Shot at low angle (camera nearly on the ground) to maximize the puddle reflection. Slightly wide angle (24mm equivalent). 8K detail in both worlds.
```

### 143. Nano Banana 2 的图表风格提示词

**Author**: [ケンイチ | AIスキルアカデミー『誰でもわかるAI活用術』](https://x.com/ChatgptAIskill)  **Date**: 2026-04-01  **Language**: ja

### 159. Nano Banana Pro 自我介绍卡生成提示词

**Author**: [貴朱音（たかね）📸 むちこ](https://x.com/ShynUrab70521)  **Date**: 2026-03-31  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 nano banana 图像生成模型设计的详细结构化提示词模板，用于创建“自我介绍卡”图像。它指定了格式、文本字段（姓名、家庭、爱好、性格等）、字体样式、调色板和装饰元素，以实现“梦幻可爱”（Yumekawa）和少女感的审美风格。

![Nano Banana Pro 自我介绍卡生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775026365180_zwse4r_HExDlwsaoAABrCX.jpg)

```
format: "self_intro_sheet"
text:
  title: "自己紹介シート"
  fields:
    名前: "{argument name="名前" default="おなまえ"}"
    家族: "{argument name="家族" default="お父さん、お母さん、妹"}"
    血液型: "A型"
    趣味: "カフェめぐり、写真を撮ること"
    性格: "明るい、よく笑う、マイペース"
    休日は: "友だちとお出かけしたり、かわいいお店を探したりする"
    好きな物: "プリン、いちご、かわいい服、おしゃれなカフェ"
    好みのタイプ: "やさしくて思いやりがある人"
    嫌いな物: "苦いもの"
    一言メッセージ: "仲よくしてくれるとうれしいです"

font:
  title: "ふんわりした太めの丸文字"
  label: "やさしい手書き風"
  body: "ポップな読みやすい丸文字"
  color: "ピンク色"

vibe:
  overall: "ゆめかわ、ガーリー、やさしくて甘い雰囲気"
  colors:
    - "ピンク"
    - "ラベンダー"
    - "ベビーブルー"
  decorations:
    - "犬"
    - "熊"
    - "ライオン"
    - "猫"

"A young woman with long wavy red hair and fair skin with a natural glow is sitting barefoot on a glossy white marble countertop in a modern interior. She wears a sleeveless form-fitting red dress that ends above the knee. Her body is angled slightly toward the camera as she looks directly at the viewer with a soft expression, one finger gently touching her lips in a thoughtful pose. Her left leg is bent with the knee raised and her right leg extended forward, foot resting on the counter. A pair of shiny silver high-heeled sandals lies on the countertop beside her feet. Image 2 prompt:

Her right hand rests on her raised left knee as she leans slightly forward, gazing at the camera with a subtle smile. Her legs are crossed at the ankles with one knee bent. The setting includes a dark staircase with black railings in the background. Even lighting creates a glossy highlight on her skin and the polished marble surface, emphasizing the elegant and confident pose."

Image 3 prompt:

"A young woman with long straight red hair and fair skin sits on a glossy white marble countertop in a fitted sleeveless red dress. She wears matching silver high-heeled sandals with ankle straps on both feet, which are positioned prominently in the foreground. Image 4 prompt:

She wears silver high-heeled sandals with thin straps and ankle cuffs on both feet. One leg is bent with the knee raised while the other is extended, and her hands rest casually on her leg and the counter for support. She looks at the camera with a gentle smile and slightly tilted head. The background consists of a dark staircase with black railings in a contemporary home setting. Soft professional lighting creates attractive highlights on her skin and the shiny marble surface."

### 169. 适用于 Gemini (Nano Banana) 的 VTuber 与街头风格 Logo 提示词

An artistic monochrome typographic illustration where the single word "CAT" appears only once and becomes a stretching domestic cat, low in front with hindquarters slightly raised and the tail extending backward in a graceful arc. ### 177. Artemis II 任务日志立体模型

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-03-31  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 设计的复杂结构化提示词，采用类 Python 的类定义，旨在生成 Artemis II 任务中宇航员任务规划日志的超精细立体模型可视化效果，重点展示从 2D 草图到物理 3D 微缩模型的演变过程。

![Artemis II 任务日志立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775026348576_nceyfl_HEso4rBacAA3ZI3.jpg)
![Artemis II 任务日志立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775026348582_fruhxc_HEso3CkagAAKgQD.jpg)

```
do this for Artemis II mission: class Artemis_Journal_Diorama:
    def __init__(self, subject="Artemis II Mission"):
        # AI infers the correct materials, textures, and desk environment
        self.stage = "AI‑inferred astronaut’s mission‑planning journal lying open on an AI‑inferred technical workstation."
        self. lighting = "AI‑inferred mixed illumination: task‑lamp warmth + cool instrument‑panel spill."

    def semantic_2D_to_3D_growth(self):
        # AI infers what '2D mission sketches' look like for this subject
        page_texture = (
            f"AI‑inferred handwritten notes, trajectory arcs, module schematics, "
            f"and mission annotations related to {self.subject}, rendered as precise 2D graphite diagrams."
        )

        # AI infers what physical 3D elements should emerge from those sketches
        diorama_pop = (
            f"2D mission diagrams transition into physical 3D miniatures: "
            f"AI‑inferred spacecraft components, crew figures, lunar geometry, "
            f"and mission‑specific hardware rising seamlessly from the paper."
        )

        return [page_texture, diorama_pop]

    def scatter_ephemera(self):
        # AI infers mission‑relevant desk objects without hard‑coding categories
        return infer_aerospace_ephemera(self.subject)
        # Examples (AI‑inferred, not fixed): mission patches, navigation tools,
        # micro‑scale lunar models, printed telemetry, procedural checklists,
        # archival headlines, engineering pencils, etc.

render(Artemis_Journal_Diorama())
```
